width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;608&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"608\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-d5f016829bd6b662599f66771f602df7_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-d5f016829bd6b662599f66771f602df7_b.jpg\"/></figure><ul><li>宋体字和街舞的气质不符，显得比较传统</li><li>图片的摆放比较突兀，排版随意</li><li>内页的文案集中在一段，不易阅读</li></ul><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>▶ 美化后：</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-8b22cfd8a772eb95693a1bdda8288044_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"608\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-8b22cfd8a772eb95693a1bdda8288044_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;608&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"608\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-8b22cfd8a772eb95693a1bdda8288044_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-8b22cfd8a772eb95693a1bdda8288044_b.jpg\"/></figure><ul><li>更换成无衬线现代体，做了倾斜处理，营造出动感</li><li>风格采用了潮流的赛博朋克风格，突显出街舞表达自我的个性</li><li>文案做了拆分处理，突出了阅读重点</li></ul><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>案例2</b></p><p>▶ 美化前：</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-62a80b60a051c58489a00e08783bdb34_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"608\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-62a80b60a051c58489a00e08783bdb34_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;608&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"608\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-62a80b60a051c58489a00e08783bdb34_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-62a80b60a051c58489a00e08783bdb34_b.jpg\"/></figure><ul><li>整体设计缺乏美感，主题风格不贴合内容</li><li>封面的设计：文字排版比较单调，标题文字不突出</li><li>内页排版设计比较粗糙，简单的文字排列，缺乏层次感</li></ul><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>▶ 美化后：</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-da2ac09c8dbde29a95b755aa18158d7a_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"608\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-da2ac09c8dbde29a95b755aa18158d7a_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;608&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"608\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-da2ac09c8dbde29a95b755aa18158d7a_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-da2ac09c8dbde29a95b755aa18158d7a_b.jpg\"/></figure><ul><li>整体排版设计采用科技风，对文字排版进行美化</li><li>采用全图形的设计，用科技元素做封面设计</li><li>内页文字的排版，加上科技元素突出文字排版</li></ul><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>案例3</b></p><p>▶ 美化前：</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-5007795401a34d67749baec8ca86d8a7_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"608\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-5007795401a34d67749baec8ca86d8a7_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;608&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"608\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-5007795401a34d67749baec8ca86d8a7_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-5007795401a34d67749baec8ca86d8a7_b.jpg\"/></figure><ul><li>文字识别性差，阅读困难</li><li>配图随意，直接摆放显得突兀</li><li>排版不够平衡，没做到对齐</li><li>背景和文字无关，且风格陈旧，活力不足</li><li>内页的内容过于紧凑，阅读压力大</li></ul><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>▶ 美化后：</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-bc78cbfc680df473d095ad911ef7914a_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"608\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-bc78cbfc680df473d095ad911ef7914a_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;608&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"608\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-bc78cbfc680df473d095ad911ef7914a_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-bc78cbfc680df473d095ad911ef7914a_b.jpg\"/></figure><ul><li>更换成思源宋体，符合文学社的国风气质</li><li>背景用了水墨烟雨渲染出国风氛围</li><li>采用居中型排版，视觉做到均衡</li><li>对内页的文案进行了拆分，减轻阅读压力</li></ul><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>案例4</b></p><p>▶ 美化前：</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-5bd47a597c4462b744f10ebdda8b7396_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"608\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-5bd47a597c4462b744f10ebdda8b7396_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;608&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"608\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-5bd47a597c4462b744f10ebdda8b7396_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-5bd47a597c4462b744f10ebdda8b7396_b.jpg\"/></figure><ul><li>整体采用设计只有一个背景图，比较单调缺乏设计感</li><li>内页文字都是大段的堆积，文字的排版没有层次，会导致阅读疲劳</li></ul><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>▶ 美化后：</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-eab1d5e3c9b14173ca6bd28ba2601ad7_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"609\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-eab1d5e3c9b14173ca6bd28ba2601ad7_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;609&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"609\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-eab1d5e3c9b14173ca6bd28ba2601ad7_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-eab1d5e3c9b14173ca6bd28ba2601ad7_b.jpg\"/></figure><ul><li>采用质感油彩画的元素做设计，提升整体设计感</li><li>对文字内容进行梳理排版，区分标题和内容增加层次感，让文字更容易阅读理解</li></ul><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-7b79780b46821cb2b15c30fc6822b1a2_b.png\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"157\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-7b79780b46821cb2b15c30fc6822b1a2_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1097&#39; height=&#39;620&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1097\" data-rawheight=\"620\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1097\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-3bd64bbe2bb9d3de00a7bfaf4c9ab676_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-3bd64bbe2bb9d3de00a7bfaf4c9ab676_b.jpg\"/></figure><p><b>注意点：</b></p><p>1、使用线条做视觉引导时，需遵循人正常视觉流向，尽量从上到下，从左到右进行引导；</p><p>2、避免引导线条过多，让观众视觉混乱，眼睛不知道该往哪里瞟，最后适得其反。<br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-38205d9a446f9f9e343983bcc1bff9b9_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1306\" data-rawheight=\"352\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1306\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-38205d9a446f9f9e343983bcc1bff9b9_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"854\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-9f9da7d7ebc4533c95ca8590ec2d8160_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;854&#39; height=&#39;484&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"854\" data-rawheight=\"484\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"854\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-9f9da7d7ebc4533c95ca8590ec2d8160_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-9f9da7d7ebc4533c95ca8590ec2d8160_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>如果对单纯的矩形图片感到乏味，想要来点<b>“高级”玩法</b>，我们还能对图片进行一下简单的处理</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><h2>■ <b>方法1</b>：形状裁剪</h2><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-e9fa977e814615c4142c1a427113312c_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"10000\" data-rawheight=\"5626\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"10000\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-e9fa977e814615c4142c1a427113312c_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;10000&#39; height=&#39;5626&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"10000\" data-rawheight=\"5626\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"10000\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-e9fa977e814615c4142c1a427113312c_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-e9fa977e814615c4142c1a427113312c_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>图片的裁切有多种方法，最简单的是系统自带的裁切。利用PPT自带的图片裁剪工具、<b>可将图片裁剪为圆形、三角形、五边形、六边形等等。</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>裁剪出来的图片形状多样，提供了更多的美化空间，不同的版式设计。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-ffe4871b25e157d6c2d104f767ece398_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"697\" data-rawheight=\"394\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"697\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-ffe4871b25e157d6c2d104f767ece398_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;697&#39; height=&#39;394&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"697\" data-rawheight=\"394\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"697\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-ffe4871b25e157d6c2d104f767ece398_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-ffe4871b25e157d6c2d104f767ece398_b.jpg\"/></figure><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-1a9a5701602da84c8b0c5b87047a18e3_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"608\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-1a9a5701602da84c8b0c5b87047a18e3_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;608&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"608\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-1a9a5701602da84c8b0c5b87047a18e3_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-1a9a5701602da84c8b0c5b87047a18e3_b.jpg\"/></figure><p><b>操作步骤：</b>在PPT中双击图片 →点击工具栏中的“裁剪”→“裁剪为形状”→ 选择形状即可  </p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><h2>■ <b>方法2</b>：切图</h2><p>如果觉得形状裁剪可选的形状过于简单，我们还可以先<b>将形状进行组合</b>，在产生新的形状之后，再来填充图片。</p><p>如此一来，就能够创造出更多丰富的图片造型</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-eba659b3ef2d6043eb178bfbc0994c49_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"13332\" data-rawheight=\"3134\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"13332\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-eba659b3ef2d6043eb178bfbc0994c49_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=\"13332\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-eba659b3ef2d6043eb178bfbc0994c49_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-eba659b3ef2d6043eb178bfbc0994c49_b.jpg\"/></figure><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-3f2dcd7a9d27edf01e7acbe0393ba7ce_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1196\" data-rawheight=\"675\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1196\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-3f2dcd7a9d27edf01e7acbe0393ba7ce_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1196\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-3f2dcd7a9d27edf01e7acbe0393ba7ce_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-3f2dcd7a9d27edf01e7acbe0393ba7ce_b.jpg\"/></figure><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a42a9f0b08d8ac15efb84f53c97e7dad_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1193\" data-rawheight=\"673\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a42a9f0b08d8ac15efb84f53c97e7dad_b.jpg\"/></figure><p><b>操作步骤：</b>在PPT中插入多个形状 → 形状边框选择“无轮廓”→ 去除形状边框 → 组合所有形状（ctrl+G）→ 设置图片填充</p><p>当然你也可以<b>换成各种不规则的形状，</b>也可以<b>尝试用多个规则的形状拼贴</b>一张图片，这样你就可以轻松做出下面的图片效果：</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-bbb1a70363c6a08b0a13c3da634956ba_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1195\" data-rawheight=\"674\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" 整体风格不符的图片时，通过这样的方式，既能保证了PPT整体风格的和谐，还能一定程度上，增加画面层次感</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-b2cab993620c6c790d160a82a691bee3_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><h2>■ <b>方法5</b>：多图片处理</h2><p>多图片排版，是制作 PPT 的常见场景之一，几乎每个人都会碰到的。图片数量一多，很多人都不知道该如何去排版。</p><p><br/>一种最简单的基本方法，就是<b>统一</b>每张图片的大小，<b>整齐</b>的排列。多张图片排列有序，整体给人以“整齐划一”的感觉。</p><p             "content": "<p><b>字体</b>作为PPT元素之一，稍不重视，就会变成“<b>灾难现场</b>”。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>文字作为PPT传递信息的重要载体，<b>应该如何高效使用？不同场合字体的使用，有什么需要注意的呢？</b></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-7f603791ae0648b8741afc8b368cba17_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"10000\" data-rawheight=\"5626\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-7e22d78f074d9e95a7ee33a80101c698_b.jpg\"/></figure><h2><b>字体的分类</b></h2><p><b>字体有很多种，但大体的类别有：</b></p><ul><li>衬线体（serif）</li><li>无衬线体（sanserif）</li><li>手写体（script）</li></ul><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-ef6bfbfd656bd5deae10247554860d14_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"10000\" data-rawheight=\"5626\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"10000\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-ef6bfbfd656bd5deae10247554860d14_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;10000&#39; height=&#39;5626&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"10000\" data-rawheight=\"5626\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"10000\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-ef6bfbfd656bd5deae10247554860d14_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-ef6bfbfd656bd5deae10247554860d14_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><ul><li><b>衬线体</b></li></ul><p><b>定义：</b>笔画末端有爪状或者线条的字体，如宋体</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-1064a0a15399a1e8dce8e5b87c3b4fbb_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"10000\" data-rawheight=\"5626\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"10000\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-1064a0a15399a1e8dce8e5b87c3b4fbb_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;10000&#39; height=&#39;5626&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"10000\" data-rawheight=\"5626\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"10000\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-1064a0a15399a1e8dce8e5b87c3b4fbb_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-1064a0a15399a1e8dce8e5b87c3b4fbb_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><ul><li><b>无衬线体</b></li></ul><p><b>定义：</b>与衬线字体相反，该类字体通常是机械的和统一线条的，它们往往拥有相同的曲率，笔直的线条，锐利的转角，如黑体</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-19947b07d7a8334ccd41175083797000_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"10000\" data-rawheight=\"5626\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"10000\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-19947b07d7a8334ccd41175083797000_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;10000&#39; height=&#39;5626&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"10000\" data-rawheight=\"5626\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"10000\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-19947b07d7a8334ccd41175083797000_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-19947b07d7a8334ccd41175083797000_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>大多数人制作幻灯片时，在字体的选择和使用上往往会使用系统默认“宋体”。但是却忽略了其识别度却不够高的弱点。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-5ff1dca5a85a115efc33d8f150eda1ff_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1410\" data-rawheight=\"793\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-43632bda8addbd13cb1be8472a4f2d0b_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1410\" data-rawheight=\"793\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1410\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-43632bda8addbd13cb1be8472a4f2d0b_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1410\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-43632bda8addbd13cb1be8472a4f2d0b_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-43632bda8addbd13cb1be8472a4f2d0b_b.jpg\"/></figure><p><b>相对于宋体，选择微软雅黑作为主要的字体是比较安全的做法。</b>无论是严肃还是活泼， 无论是正文还是标题，使用这个字体，阅读都非常方便 ，而且所有电脑上都有这个字体，不会出现幻灯片演示当天字体丢失或变形的尴尬情况。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>不过需要注意的是，<b>微软雅黑为不可商用字体</b>，使用时需要多加注意。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-4ebaf9c15b414abe49f6d71a478f7d61_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"168\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-4ebaf9c15b414abe49f6d71a478f7d61_b.jpg\"/></figure><h2><b>清晰明了，风格统一</b></h2><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>对于PPT字体的选择，切不可“随心情”。实际上，<b>一些字体虽然艺术感十足，但是用在PPT上面则较难辨认</b>；如果运用到正文中很可能会影响阅读效果</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img width=&#39;10000&#39; height=&#39;5625&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"10000\" data-rawheight=\"5625\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"10000\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-f6061c65578e80ce87568334e3578fd6_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-f6061c65578e80ce87568334e3578fd6_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>PPT最后一页，一般大家都会以<b>“谢谢”，“感谢观看”，“Thanks”</b>作为结束语。但是观众看多了也会有视觉疲劳，甚至还会觉得有点俗套。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-bced60f404dedfafd9a2c5799eca5af7_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"10000\" data-rawheight=\"5625\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"10000\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-bced60f404dedfafd9a2c5799eca5af7_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;10000&#39; height=&#39;5625&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"10000\" data-rawheight=\"5625\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"10000\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-bced60f404dedfafd9a2c5799eca5af7_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-bced60f404dedfafd9a2c5799eca5af7_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>那么除了以上结束语，PPT结束页还能有什么“新玩法”？</b></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-fefa8f6a53a12d398414f02620647c94_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"10000\" data-rawheight=\"5625\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"10000\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-fefa8f6a53a12d398414f02620647c94_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;10000&#39; height=&#39;5625&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"10000\" data-rawheight=\"5625\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"10000\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-fefa8f6a53a12d398414f02620647c94_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-fefa8f6a53a12d398414f02620647c94_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><h2>以下总结5种既得体，又能瞬间逼格满满的结束页创意方式</h2><p><b>附上适用场合</b></p><p><b>绝对能让你PPT格调 up up up!</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><h2>1、传达特定信息</h2><p><b>（1）联系方式</b></p><p>适用场合：商业会议、路演融资等较为正式的场合</p><p>在PPT结束页留下联系信息（公司地址/官网网址/官微二维码/邮箱等其他联系信息）</p><p>在体现专业性的同时，也能够达到宣传转化的目的。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-0194e8c0bbc7bdd8eb2af2095ade2f93_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"10000\" data-rawheight=\"5625\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"10000\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-0194e8c0bbc7bdd8eb2af2095ade2f93_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;10000&#39; height=&#39;5625&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"10000\" data-rawheight=\"5625\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"10000\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-0194e8c0bbc7bdd8eb2af2095ade2f93_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-0194e8c0bbc7bdd8eb2af2095ade2f93_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>（2）Q&amp;A</b></p><p>适用场合：有提问环节的场合</p><p>如分享会、学术会议等教育知识相关的，甚至是公司入职培训亦同样适用</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-74472297124535dbdc682648bdb04880_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"10000\" data-rawheight=\"5625\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"10000\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-74472297124535dbdc682648bdb04880_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;10000&#39; height=&#39;5625&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"10000\" data-rawheight=\"5625\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"10000\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-74472297124535dbdc682648bdb04880_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-74472297124535dbdc682648bdb04880_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>（3）号召行动</b></p><ul><li><b>表达意愿，招聘/招商</b></li></ul><p>适用场合：招聘宣讲会，企业招商会</p><p>当你在做一场校园招聘宣讲会，演讲结束时，展现这样一版结束页，绝对会比单纯的“谢谢观看”来的更有号召力。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-d42b082578f63a9762993cd2e1a2819c_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"10000\" data-rawheight=\"5625\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"10000\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-d42b082578f63a9762993cd2e1a2819c_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;10000&#39; height=&#39;5625&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"10000\" data-rawheight=\"5625\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"10000\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-87eb93e0d60453ee9ba56c6798181c14_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-87eb93e0d60453ee9ba56c6798181c14_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><h2>2、品牌宣传</h2><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-294fb2a32851ddcfd03fdd17299eafad_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"10000\" data-rawheight=\"5625\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"10000\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-294fb2a32851ddcfd03fdd17299eafad_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;10000&#39; height=&#39;5625&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"10000\" data-rawheight=\"5625\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"10000\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-fc41b296cdff0f822c3c1ff47a653829_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-fc41b296cdff0f822c3c1ff47a653829_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><h2>3、传达情感</h2><p><b>适用场合：发布会、演讲、目的性会议</b></p><p><b>作为PPT的封底，我们可以以表达情感/情怀的金句作为结束语</b></p><p>一方面能够传达演讲者的核心价值观，另一方面也能够抒发情怀，引发观众共鸣，激发行动。通过强化观点/主题，进而达到PPT讲演的目的。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-9250b95d4c7c674ca89242897098a4d3_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"10000\" data-rawheight=\"5625\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"10000\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-9250b95d4c7c674ca89242897098a4d3_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;10000&#39; height=&#39;5625&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"10000\" data-rawheight=\"5625\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"10000\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-9250b95d4c7c674ca89242897098a4d3_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-9250b95d4c7c674ca89242897098a4d3_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><h2>4、总结回顾</h2><p><b>适用场合：课堂教学、知识分享</b></p><p>通过总结全篇内容，给观看者进行简单内容回顾</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-43cb6749c7e051811a6dba0097ddda98_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"10000\" data-rawheight=\"5625\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"10000\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-43cb6749c7e051811a6dba0097ddda98_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;10000&#39; height=&#39;5625&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"10000\" data-rawheight=\"5625\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"10000\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-43cb6749c7e051811a6dba0097ddda98_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-43cb6749c7e051811a6dba0097ddda98_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><h2>5、幽默创意型</h2><p><b>适用场合：非正式场合</b></p><p>当观众长时间精神聚焦在枯燥乏味的PPT报告时，身体难免“被催眠”。</p><p>这时候我们可以尝试用轻松幽默的方式，来个趣味结尾活跃一下气氛，让观众眼前一亮，留下深刻印象。如果在PPT中可以有一个有趣的结尾，一定会让你在整个演讲中令人眼前一亮，在戏谑中活跃气氛。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-b7b94d6baed3ca2f831528f4fa214371_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"10000\" data-rawheight=\"5625\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"10000\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-b7b94d6baed3ca2f831528f4fa214371_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;10000&#39; height=&#39;5625&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"10000\" data-rawheight=\"5625\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"10000\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-b7b94d6baed3ca2f831528f4fa214371_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-b7b94d6baed3ca2f831528f4fa214371_b.jpg\"/></figure><h2>第二部分：呈现方式</h2><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-8be71b7bf775f07c08298e834bc8f6f9_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"10000\" data-rawheight=\"5625\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"10000\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-8be71b7bf775f07c08298e834bc8f6f9_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;             "content": "<p>在实际工作中，很多人可能习惯性将PPT作为演示版的Word来使用。文字排版毫无美感，内容堆砌主次不分。一大段文字密密麻麻，让人顿时没了继续观看下去的欲望。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-cc89a3cb7e4e42b40a30589a0d2a24d3_b.jpg\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"830\" data-rawheight=\"467\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"830\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-cc89a3cb7e4e42b40a30589a0d2a24d3_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;720&#39; height=&#39;405&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"720\" data-rawheight=\"405\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"720\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-08b6acd49b506d74c91c1358bd9051f7_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-08b6acd49b506d74c91c1358bd9051f7_b.jpg\"/></figure><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-d9a8814cb8d94848dfdbfef6e8373df1_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"3000\" data-rawheight=\"1687\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"3000\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-d9a8814cb8d94848dfdbfef6e8373df1_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;3000&#39; height=&#39;1687&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"3000\" data-rawheight=\"1687\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"3000\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-5d6e62e179264240a9ebbcd4354ce614_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-5d6e62e179264240a9ebbcd4354ce614_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>如何摆脱“LOW”排版？快速做出内容排版清晰，主次分明的PPT？</b></p><h2><b>以下4个小技巧能帮到你</b></h2><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-45987eb604d126cfa7beafd068284170_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"3000\" data-rawheight=\"1687\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"3000\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-45987eb604d126cfa7beafd068284170_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;3000&#39; height=&#39;1687&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"3000\" data-rawheight=\"1687\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"3000\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-45987eb604d126cfa7beafd068284170_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-45987eb604d126cfa7beafd068284170_b.jpg\"/></figure><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b157e630c5cfdc18c5c02b09d33d7796_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"3000\" data-rawheight=\"1687\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"3000\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b157e630c5cfdc18c5c02b09d33d7796_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;3000&#39; height=&#39;1687&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"3000\" data-rawheight=\"1687\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"3000\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b157e630c5cfdc18c5c02b09d33d7796_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b157e630c5cfdc18c5c02b09d33d7796_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>通过上图PPT案例展示，我们可以看到，<b>一大段文字堆砌，字体颜色过多，字体不统一，造成观看者阅读压力，让人容易抓不到内容的重点。</b></p><h2>1、统一字体，拆分文案</h2><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-bff2309ff6ee122734cc8e48e20af504_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"3000\" data-rawheight=\"1687\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"3000\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-bff2309ff6ee122734cc8e48e20af504_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;3000&#39; height=&#39;1687&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"3000\" data-rawheight=\"1687\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"3000\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-bff2309ff6ee122734cc8e48e20af504_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-bff2309ff6ee122734cc8e48e20af504_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>统一字体能够更方便读者阅读。根据PPT内容进行文案拆分，避免一大段文字堆砌，这样也有助于内容的清晰呈现。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><h2>2、有意识突出重要信息</h2><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-241e5097b201fcbfe95d20a622ee7613_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"3000\" data-rawheight=\"1687\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"3000\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-241e5097b201fcbfe95d20a622ee7613_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;3000&#39; height=&#39;1687&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"3000\" data-rawheight=\"1687\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"3000\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-241e5097b201fcbfe95d20a622ee7613_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-241e5097b201fcbfe95d20a622ee7613_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>对于重要的内容信息，我们可以选择用不同颜色或者色块作为区分/突出。不过要注意的是，字体颜色最好不要超过3种，过多的颜色也会加重读者阅读负担。</p><h2>3、根据内容配图</h2><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-da817a04611e7791f47ba9293e74eedc_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"3000\" data-rawheight=\"1687\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"3000\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-da817a04611e7791f47ba9293e74eedc_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;3000&#39; height=&#39;1687&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"3000\" data-rawheight=\"1687\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"3000\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-da817a04611e7791f47ba9293e74eedc_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-da817a04611e7791f47ba9293e74eedc_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>纯文字的PPT容易让人抓不住重点，而根据内容需求来配图（图片/图标），一方面能够对文字内容进行区分；另一方面，也能够增加阅读“趣味性”，不会过于单调乏味。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-ad1adf42e8f523d792e93bbca43ce4a7_b.jpg\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1287\" data-rawheight=\"744\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1287\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-ad1adf42e8f523d792e93bbca43ce4a7_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1371&#39; height=&#39;774&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1371\" data-rawheight=\"774\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1371\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4145632a11465086f4b4f2a650990298_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4145632a11465086f4b4f2a650990298_b.jpg\"/><figcaption>模板源于吾道幻灯片 woodo.cn</figcaption></figure><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-c131250050641e67aef1649f1d7f2f7d_b.jpg\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1374\" data-rawheight=\"768\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1374\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-c131250050641e67aef1649f1d7f2f7d_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1374&#39; height=&#39;768&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1374\" data-rawheight=\"768\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1374\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-c131250050641e67aef1649f1d7f2f7d_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-c131250050641e67aef1649f1d7f2f7d_b.jpg\"/><figcaption>模板源于吾道幻灯片 woodo.cn</figcaption></figure><h2>4、创意排版，脑洞打开</h2><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-99fa0dc54efe313890ab987ce2ab8918_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"3000\" data-rawheight=\"1687\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"3000\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-99fa0dc54efe313890ab987ce2ab8918_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;3000&#39; height=&#39;1687&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"3000\" data-rawheight=\"1687\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"3000\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-99fa0dc54efe313890ab987ce2ab8918_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-99fa0dc54efe313890ab987ce2ab8918_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>除了一般样式的排版以外，我们还能尝试一下创意排版，不拘泥于格式的呈现。毕竟，PPT作为一个演示工具，而不是纯粹的文字承载工具。所以我们可以尝试适当删减一些文字内容，保留核心内容，把自己更多的思想留到实际讲演的那一天，这样也能避免照着PPT念稿的尴尬现象。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-2d6b27de33e7360c3f1c7c3a2be95d45_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"3000\" data-rawheight=\"1687\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"3000\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-2d6b27de33e7360c3f1c7c3a2be95d45_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;3000&#39; height=&#39;1687&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"3000\" data-rawheight=\"1687\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"3000\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-2d6b27de33e7360c3f1c7c3a2be95d45_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-2d6b27de33e7360c3f1c7c3a2be95d45_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>最后我们来总结一下图文排版4个简单的小技巧</b></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-66928444a0abd674c88dba897cf46a0a_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"3000\" data-rawheight=\"1687\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"3000\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-66928444a0abd674c88dba897cf46a0a_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;             "title": "吾道系列 | PPT目录页太单调？5大版式轻松学起来！", 
            "content": "<p><b>目录页作为整个PPT框架梳理，能够让制作者循着逻辑思路进行内容呈现设计</b>，避免思路过于天马行空；另一方面<b>可以让观看者对接下来讲的内容有大致的了解</b>。所以，制作一个清晰美观的PPT目录就显得特别重要。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>高赞回答对PPT目录设计已经讲解得十分透彻。但是相信很多人做PPT都不是常规性工作，<b>如何在最短的时间内做出一个美观清晰的目录页呢？</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-12bbeb08b3fb85eada132f828f89b454_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" class=\"content_image\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;0&#39; height=&#39;0&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" class=\"content_image lazy\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-12bbeb08b3fb85eada132f828f89b454_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-64ec8de4a296a90eb3c9bb7ae8777424_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"608\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-64ec8de4a296a90eb3c9bb7ae8777424_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;608&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"608\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-64ec8de4a296a90eb3c9bb7ae8777424_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-64ec8de4a296a90eb3c9bb7ae8777424_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>实际上，<b>目录页影响的是整个PPT的逻辑结构。</b>说具体点，<b>它的作用</b>是：<b>内容逻辑的体现，</b>将内容划分为多个板块，每个总结为一个章节标题。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>一个好的PPT目录能够清晰地表达内容从总到分的逻辑过渡</b>，能让观众了解到整个PPT内容框架，从而达到更好的演示效果。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4abe2695fe6c0ad03825b4b67728667c_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"608\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4abe2695fe6c0ad03825b4b67728667c_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;658&#39; height=&#39;370&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"658\" data-rawheight=\"370\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"658\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-da53463fc60118779e801b0e9af79364_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-da53463fc60118779e801b0e9af79364_b.jpg\"/></figure><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-6ae2a5bb7188b62aae60cbbab13a9630_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"658\" data-rawheight=\"370\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"658\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-6ae2a5bb7188b62aae60cbbab13a9630_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;658&#39; height=&#39;370&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"658\" data-rawheight=\"370\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"658\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-2057dd2ae302650456ef918c46981d89_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-2057dd2ae302650456ef918c46981d89_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><h2><b>Part 1 目录组成</b></h2><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-476d8482b33c587d46255b16e3bd82e9_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"608\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-476d8482b33c587d46255b16e3bd82e9_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;608&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"608\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-476d8482b33c587d46255b16e3bd82e9_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-476d8482b33c587d46255b16e3bd82e9_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>目录页主要由<b>序号</b>、<b>章节标题、目录标识</b>三个元素构成。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-fffb84474f841a7f3ca5943421b8dbb1_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"889\" data-rawheight=\"370\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"889\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-fffb84474f841a7f3ca5943421b8dbb1_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;889&#39; height=&#39;370&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"889\" data-rawheight=\"370\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"889\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-fffb84474f841a7f3ca5943421b8dbb1_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-fffb84474f841a7f3ca5943421b8dbb1_b.jpg\"/></figure><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-ad0a596157a33cea4a30ef0e09c31f90_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"608\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-ad0a596157a33cea4a30ef0e09c31f90_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;608&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"608\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-ad0a596157a33cea4a30ef0e09c31f90_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-ad0a596157a33cea4a30ef0e09c31f90_b.jpg\"/></figure><ul><li><b>目录标识：</b></li></ul><p>主要围绕“目录”两字进行修饰设计，简单的设计能够防止页面单调。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><ul><li><b>序 号：</b></li></ul><p>对多个内容板块作一个排列顺序，一般使用数字，也可以使用小图标 代替。 通过各种形状、图标、素材的组合，可以玩出很多种形式的章节序号。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><ul><li><b>章节标题：</b></li></ul><p>将内容划分为多个板块，并对每个板块做总结归纳的一个标题。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-d120be9cbc4126dc506469b6023e78cc_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"586\" data-rawheight=\"39\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"586\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-d120be9cbc4126dc506469b6023e78cc_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;586&#39; height=&#39;39&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"586\" data-rawheight=\"39\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"586\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-d120be9cbc4126dc506469b6023e78cc_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-d120be9cbc4126dc506469b6023e78cc_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><h2><b>Part 2 设计原则</b></h2><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><ul><li><b>版式统一</b></li></ul><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-c677487b1d3c5cc44cf19d15254d1d91_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"608\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-c677487b1d3c5cc44cf19d15254d1d91_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;608&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"608\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-c677487b1d3c5cc44cf19d15254d1d91_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-c677487b1d3c5cc44cf19d15254d1d91_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>顾名思义，就是<b>标题所涉及的元素要做到一致。</b>无论是形状的使用，还是英文搭配，细到对齐字体距离等等。</p><p>有的小伙伴在写标题的时候，喜欢<b>在一个文本框内把所有章节标题写进去</b>，其实这是<b>不利于我们进行二次排版设计的</b>。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><ul><li><b>等距对齐</b></li></ul><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-34a3a1ee516577d1bc3f6ef40b6a7497_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"608\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-34a3a1ee516577d1bc3f6ef40b6a7497_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;608&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"608\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-34a3a1ee516577d1bc3f6ef40b6a7497_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-34a3a1ee516577d1bc3f6ef40b6a7497_b.jpg\"/></figure><p><b>等距</b>包括<b>每个序号章节标题间的距离</b>。</p><p>将大标题和小标题之间的距离等距以后，目录排版会很整齐，很舒服，阅读起来也很省力。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-d120be9cbc4126dc506469b6023e78cc_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"586\" data-rawheight=\"39\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"586\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-d120be9cbc4126dc506469b6023e78cc_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;586&#39; height=&#39;39&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"586\" data-rawheight=\"39\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"586\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-d120be9cbc4126dc506469b6023e78cc_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-d120be9cbc4126dc506469b6023e78cc_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><h2><b>Part 3 常见目录版式</b></h2><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-c394a52d015e363c56e5a854de6bf2b6_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"608\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-c394a52d015e363c56e5a854de6bf2b6_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;608&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"608\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-c394a52d015e363c56e5a854de6bf2b6_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-c394a52d015e363c56e5a854de6bf2b6_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><ul><li><b>左右排列</b></li></ul><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-7c43f2fe856e067f1ab5338b016203a5_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"608\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-7c43f2fe856e067f1ab5338b016203a5_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;608&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"608\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-f179c334247c2ba232b7adcfaf9c572e_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-f179c334247c2ba232b7adcfaf9c572e_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>使用<b>圆形，矩形，正方形</b>等<b>多种形状填充</b>，多使用并排分布，配合小图标更有效果。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-d120be9cbc4126dc506469b6023e78cc_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"586\" data-rawheight=\"39\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"586\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-d120be9cbc4126dc506469b6023e78cc_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;586&#39; height=&#39;39&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"586\" data-rawheight=\"39\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"586\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-d120be9cbc4126dc506469b6023e78cc_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-d120be9cbc4126dc506469b6023e78cc_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><h2><b>Part 4 教程总结</b></h2><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b637d940b9852482db83e3b0f5b43596_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"608\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b637d940b9852482db83e3b0f5b43596_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;608&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"608\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b637d940b9852482db83e3b0f5b43596_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b637d940b9852482db83e3b0f5b43596_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>最后，我们来做个<b>简单的总结：</b></p><ul><li><b>目录组成</b>：目录标识、序号、章节标题</li><li><b>排版原则</b>：版式统一、等距对齐</li><li><b>常见版式</b>：上下排列、左右排列、斜块排列、多形状排列、创意型设计<br/></li></ul><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><h2><b>以上教程完整发布于「吾道共享作品」：</b><br/><b><a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//www.woodo.cn/mobile/slides/%3Fid%3D349\" class=\" external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\"><span class=\"invisible\">https://www.</span><span class=\"visible\">woodo.cn/mobile/slides/?</span><span class=\"invisible\">id=349</span><span class=\"ellipsis\"></span></a></b></h2><h2><b>感兴趣的同学，点击链接即可跳转观看收藏学习喔~</b></h2><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-d120be9cbc4126dc506469b6023e78cc_b.png\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"586\" data-rawheight=\"39\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"586\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-d120be9cbc4126dc506469b6023e78cc_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;
